### [402] [When AI Is Wrong on Purpose: How Students Respond to Buggy GenAI Code](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05068)
*Victor-Alexandru Pădurean,Kaitlin Riegel,Alkis Gotovos,Jyotika Mahapatra,Ahana Ghosh,Paul Denny,Juho Leinonen,James Prather,Adish Singla*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本研究探索在CS1教学中，通过向GenAI生成的正确代码中注入真实可运行故障，促使学生进行代码审查与修复。分析917名学生2636次交互发现，注入的bug更多引发直接代码编辑，而提示相关失败则促使学生优化提示词。学生反馈表明这种方法有助于培养代码理解、审查和调试能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GenAI在编程教育中日益普及，但学生往往缺乏对生成代码进行审慎验证的动机，因为当前模型常能正确完成任务。如何设计提示为中心的编程活动，以更好地培养学生的代码审查和验证能力，是本研究要解决的核心问题。

Method: 在CS1编程活动中，向原本正确的GenAI生成代码中故意注入真实可运行的bug，对比分析自然产生的提示相关失败与故意注入bug两种情况下学生的行为差异。收集了917名学生的2636次编程会话数据进行分析。

Result: 学生对不同来源的bug反应不同：故意注入的bug更多导致直接代码编辑和更高的下次尝试成功率；提示相关失败则更多促使学生通过优化提示词来解决问题。学生反馈认为这种设计有助于提升代码理解、审查和调试能力，并培养更谨慎的验证心态。

Conclusion: 提示相关的失败和故意注入的bug共同支持了具有教学价值的GenAI工作流，学生既能通过提示词练习需求精化，又能通过代码编辑练习调试，两者相辅相成。

Abstract: As Generative AI (GenAI) becomes increasingly central to software development, CS education is integrating prompt-centered workflows where students describe intended program behavior in natural language to elicit code. However, professional practice requires careful review and verification of GenAI-generated code that may appear correct while containing subtle faults. This creates a challenge for CS1-level activities, where current models often solve tasks correctly and reduce students' incentive to closely inspect generated outputs. We investigate how prompt-centered programming activities can be adapted to better foster these practices. Specifically, we explore an approach where realistic, runnable bugs are injected into otherwise correct solutions, thus requiring students to read and repair generated outputs. We analyzed 2,636 sessions from 917 students, and examined behavior across instances of naturally occurring prompt-related failures and deliberately injected bugs within each session. Our findings show that students responded differently across bug sources. Deliberately injected bugs more often led to direct code edits and higher next-attempt success, suggesting localized repair of near-miss solutions. Prompt-related failures instead more often led students to refine prompts by clarifying constraints, updating function signatures, adding edge cases, or reframing the task. Student reflections reinforce the emphasis on review and repair, describing useful practice in code understanding, code review, and debugging, as well as a more careful verification mindset and greater awareness of GenAI limitations. Ultimately, prompt-related failures and injected bugs together support a pedagogically useful GenAI workflow, where students practice both specification refinement through prompts and debugging through code editing.

</details>


### [403] [Can Code Specify a System Precisely Enough to Formally Verify It?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05076)
*Jean-Jacques Dubray*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文评估了用大语言模型（LLM）为生产级收银系统支付流程编写形式化规约的可靠性，发现规约合同结构（而非语言）是决定可靠性的关键因素；同时揭示了模拟器与实际API之间的“关联预言机失效”问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 形式化验证很少应用于生产软件，因为编写和维护模型成本过高。探索一种低成本替代方案：用LLM根据运行时轨迹编写规约，并评估其在真实生产环境中的可靠性。

Method: 对运营中餐厅收银系统的支付流程进行审计：基于手工构建且逐行引用的模型，在精确故障模型下验证核心协议；用LLM生成规约，对比不同合同结构和语言的效果；扩展故障模型（崩溃重启、脏读、两次尝试）进行系统性测试；对比模拟器与实际API的行为差异。

Result: 核心协议正确但发现7个故障处理缺口，3个被复现为真实执行；补丁修复后重新检查又暴露了新缺陷。模拟器未检测到实际API的响应形状差异，导致整个恢复阶梯不可达。跨7个模型验证了合同结构（而非语言）主导LLM规约可靠性，但只有最强模型达到语料上限。

Conclusion: 规约的合同结构比语言对LLM生成规约的可靠性影响更大；模拟器与实际API的差异可能导致“关联预言机失效”，需警惕。更强的模型和更难的测试任务能恢复基准的区分能力。

Abstract: Formal verification is seldom applied to production software, because writing and maintaining a model has historically cost more than it returns. A companion study [1] extended SysMoBench [4] with a lower-cost alternative: specifications are graded against traces captured from the running system. It found that when large language models write the specifications, reliability is governed by the structure of the specification contract, not the language. This paper evaluates both on production software: the payment workflow of an operational restaurant point-of-sale system, which must keep the register, payment terminal, and payment processor in agreement. We report three results. First, the core protocol is correct relative to a hand-built, line-cited model under a precisely stated failure model. The audit found seven failure-handling gaps, nearly all with a common root cause; three were reproduced as real executions, and a patch closing them was re-checked with all failure gates enabled, after which a follow-up patch closed a defect the re-check itself exposed. Systematic extensions of the failure model (crash-restart, stale reads, two attempts) each found the windows they were designed to probe. Second, a single probe of the production payment sandbox exposed a response-shape divergence that makes an entire recovery ladder unreachable against the live API. The emulator-based audit could not detect it, because code and emulator share the same misreading: a correlated-oracle failure. Third, the companion study's central finding replicates across seven models from two vendors: contract structure, not language, governs what LLMs specify reliably. The replication concerns the ordering of contracts and the failure taxonomy, not the absolute level: only the strongest models reached the corpus ceiling, and the harder task restores discriminating power the benchmark had lost.

### [404] [RepoTrace: Browser-Assisted Evidence Collection for GitHub Research Datasets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05106)
*Xue Yao,Zehua Zhang,Jiatong Liu,Yongqiang Tian*

TL;DR: RepoTrace 是一个浏览器辅助研究工具，用于从 GitHub 的 issue 和 pull request 中收集证据，并将其存储在本地 SQLite 工作区中，以解决传统手动数据收集工作流中证据分散、溯源困难、难以审计等问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的手动收集 GitHub issue 和 PR 数据的工作流程中，页面证据、研究代码和决策依据分散在不同的标签页和文件中，导致数据来源难以追溯、更新难以追踪、多审阅者标注难以审计。

Method: RepoTrace 结合 Chrome 侧边栏扩展、Express 后端和 React 仪表盘，通过本地 SQLite 数据库捕获页面快照、评论、标签、笔记、筛选决策、刷新历史和范围导出，将原始证据与研究解释关联在一起。

Result: 对 20 个 Matplotlib issue 的验证实验表明，RepoTrace 成功收集了 22 个快照、38 条评论、20 条研究笔记、98 个注释、20 个筛选评审、20 个修复证据条目和 4 个模拟的未解决共识冲突。

Abstract: Empirical software engineering studies frequently build datasets from GitHub issues and pull requests. In many projects, researchers inspect pages in a browser, copy selected fields into spreadsheets, keep side notes in separate documents, and later run scripts to normalize or export the data. This workflow is flexible, but the page evidence, the research codes, and the rationale behind each decision end up spread across tabs and files, which leaves provenance, update tracking, and multi-reviewer labeling hard to audit.
  RepoTrace is a browser-assisted research tool that collects GitHub issue and pull-request evidence into a local SQLite-backed workspace. It combines a Chrome side-panel extension, an Express backend, and a React dashboard to capture page snapshots, comments, labels, notes, screening and labeling decisions, refresh history, and scoped exports, keeping the source evidence and the research interpretation linked together.
  A validation pass collected and checked 20 Matplotlib issues across two study projects. The resulting dataset preserves 22 snapshots, 38 comments, 20 research notes, 98 annotations, 20 screening reviews, 20 fix-evidence entries, and 4 simulated unresolved consensus conflicts. The results show that RepoTrace can support a complete local evidence-collection workflow for manually constructed GitHub issue and pull-request datasets.

### [405] [From Failing to Passing: Evolving Natural Language Prompt Optimization Rules for LLM Code Generation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05121)
*Amal Akli,Melissa Akli,Cedric Richter,Mike Papadakis,Yves Le Traon*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出DUALFIX，一种结合自然语言变换规则搜索与执行反馈修复的两阶段修复流水线，能够修复10-30%的代码失败案例，其中12-17%是纯执行反馈方法无法解决的，且规则可跨模型零样本迁移。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大语言模型对提示措辞高度敏感，微小的措辞变化会显著影响性能。作者想探究这种敏感性能否被反向利用——即通过变换提示的措辞来主动提升模型性能，而非被动承受其负面影响。

Method: 1) 基于搜索的方法自动发现和演化一组自然语言变换规则；2) 提出DUALFIX两阶段修复流水线：先应用演化出的变换规则修复规约层失败，再结合执行反馈修复实现层失败。

Result: 在LiveCodeBench和APPS基准上，DUALFIX修复10-30%失败案例（含执行反馈无法修复的12-17%），恢复最多30%基线失败，修复数量是Self-Fix的3-5倍；规则可跨模型零样本迁移并优于纯执行反馈方法。

Conclusion: 通过自动演化提示变换规则，可以系统性地提升代码生成模型的性能，且该方法具有通用性——规则与具体错误无关、可跨问题复用、跨模型迁移，为提示工程提供了一种自动化、可泛化的新范式。

Abstract: Large language models are known to be sensitive to prompt formulation. Even minor variations in wording can substantially degrade performance. This sensitivity reveals an opportunity: if prompt phrasing can harm performance, can it be used to improve it? To investigate this question, we introduce a search-based approach that identifies and evolves a set of natural language transformation rules with strong downstream effects on coding performance. We then propose DUALFIX, a staged repair pipeline that combines the evolved transformation rules with execution-feedback repair, addressing both specification-level and implementation-level failures. A key strength of our approach lies in its generality: the evolved rules are error-agnostic, reusable across problems, and transferable across models. We evaluate DUALFIX against execution-feedback repair baselines across three models on two challenging benchmarks, LiveCodeBench and APPS. Our results show that the evolved transformations fix from 10-30% of failing cases, including 12-17% of failures that execution-based repair alone cannot resolve. Overall, DualFix recovers up to 30% of baseline failures and fixes 3-5 times more failing cases than Self-Fix across all evaluated settings. Furthermore, we also show that rules evolved on one model transfer zero-shot to other models, outperforming execution-feedback repair without any re-optimization.

</details>


### [406] [Three-Phase Evaluation of AI-Assisted Software Development Life Cycle](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05125)
*Joshua Strubel,Professor Carrie Russell,Carson Crockett,Jason Ferraro,Nathan Londhe,Uzayr Syed,Jacob Viehe*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过对比三种AI辅助开发阶段（部分辅助、GitHub Copilot独占、AWS Kiro独占），发现更高的AI自主性可减少开发时间、提高需求符合度并降低认知负荷，但开发者挫败感略有增加。AWS Kiro阶段综合表现最优，显示工具架构本身也影响开发效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索不同AI自主性水平对软件开发生产力、需求遵循度和开发者认知负荷的影响，填补该领域系统性评估的空白。

Method: 四名开发者在三个阶段中重新实现同一全栈Web应用：部分AI辅助（GitHub Copilot）、AI独占（GitHub Copilot）、AI独占（AWS Kiro）。测量开发工时、需求符合度（RITM评分）、AI交互效率及NASA-TXL工作负荷指标。

Result: 更高的AI自主性降低了开发工作量、提高了需求符合度、减轻了主观脑力负荷，但开发者挫败感略有上升。AWS Kiro阶段在多数维度上表现最佳。

Conclusion: AI自主性提升有助于改善开发效率与体验，但工具架构本身也独立影响结果；需在自主性与开发者挫败感之间寻求平衡。

Abstract: This paper presents an exploratory evaluation of how increasing levels of AI autonomy affect software development productivity, requirement adherence, and developer cognitive workload. A team of four developers reimplemented the same full-stack web application across three sequential phases: partial AI-assisted development using GitHub Copilot, an AI-exclusive workflow using GitHub Copilot, and an AI-exclusive workflow using AWS Kiro. Evaluation metrics included development effort (hours), requirement adherence (RITM score), AI-interaction efficiency, and NASA-TLX workload measures. Across phases, higher levels of AI autonomy were associated with reduced development effort, improved requirement adherence, and lower self-reported mental workload, while developer frustration increased modestly. The AWS Kiro phase achieved the strongest overall performance on most measured dimensions, suggesting that tooling architecture may influence outcomes independently of AI autonomy level.

</details>


### [407] [On the risk of coding before testing: An empirical study on LLM-based test generation workflow](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05139)
*Michael Konstantinou,Florian Tambon,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文研究了LLM生成代码时，错误会传播到测试用例中，导致测试失效（错误实现与测试相互一致，掩盖缺陷）。独立生成测试的缺陷检出率为25%，而基于错误代码生成测试仅为14%。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 挑战"LLM生成的测试可以独立可靠地充当oracle"这一假设，探究生成代码中的错误是否会系统性地影响后续测试的生成。

Method: 通过编程任务和agentic工作流，分析生成代码与测试断言之间的一致性，重点研究"对齐失败"场景。考察不同提示策略（包括chain-of-thought）下误差传播情况，以及多步工作流中中间输出复用导致的误差传播。

Result: 错误传播普遍存在且影响显著：基于错误代码生成测试时缺陷检出率仅14%，而独立生成测试时为25%。

Conclusion: 当前LLM工作流中生成制品间缺乏独立性，严重损害了自动化测试的可靠性；同时揭示了依赖耦合生成管线的实证研究存在以前未充分探索的有效性威胁。

Abstract: Large Language Models (LLMs) are increasingly used in software engineering workflows to generate both source code and test suites. This dual capability has enabled emerging development paradigms, including test-first and agentic workflows, where a single model is producing and validating implementations. However, these approaches assume that generated tests act as independent and reliable oracles - a fundamental requirement for effective software testing. In this paper, we challenge this assumption and investigate whether LLM-generated code biases the generation of subsequent tests. We introduce and empirically study the phenomenon of error propagation, where faults in generated code are systematically replicated in associated test artifacts. This leads to cases where incorrect implementations and tests are mutually consistent, masking defects rather than revealing them. We evaluate this effect across a range of programming tasks and agentic workflows, analyzing the consistency between generated code and test assertions, with particular focus on scenarios of aligned failures. Our study examines (i) whether erroneous code artifacts bias test generation, (ii) whether such bias persists under different prompting strategies, including chain-of-thought reasoning, and (iii) how errors propagate across multi-step workflows in which intermediate outputs are reused as context. The results show that error propagation is prevalent and impactful: generating tests after faulty code significantly reduces fault detection effectiveness compared to generating tests independently (14% vs. 25%). These findings highlight a fundamental limitation of current workflows, where lack of independence between generated artifacts undermines the reliability of automated testing. Furthermore, our results expose a previously underexplored threat to validity in empirical studies relying on coupled generation pipelines.

</details>


### [408] [Intent-Based Mutation Testing: From Naturally Written Programming Intents to Mutants](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05149)
*Asma Hamidi,Ahmed Khanfir,Mike Papadakis*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文提出基于意图的变异测试方法，通过改变程序中的编程意图（而非语法）生成变异体，利用大语言模型实现，可捕获传统方法无法检测的缺陷类型，与传统变异测试互补。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统变异测试基于语法层面修改代码，难以捕获与编程意图相关的缺陷。作者希望通过对编程意图本身进行变异，生成更贴近规格说明的复杂变异体，以发现传统方法遗漏的故障类别。

Method: 使用大语言模型（LLMs）对编程意图进行变异，将变异后的意图转化为程序变异体。与传统语法级变异不同，该方法改变的是程序"想做什么"而非"怎么写"。

Result: 在29个程序上评估，生成的变异体在语法上更复杂、语义上更多样，与传统变异体语义差异显著；55%的基于意图的变异体不被传统变异体所包含（subsume）。

Conclusion: 基于意图的变异测试是传统语法级变异测试的有力补充，能够覆盖传统方法难以触及的缺陷空间。

Abstract: This paper presents intent-based mutation testing, a testing approach that generates mutations by changing the programming intents that are implemented in the programs under test. In contrast to traditional mutation testing, which changes (mutates) the way programs are written, intent mutation changes (mutates) the behavior of the programs by producing mutations that implement (slightly) different intents than those implemented in the original program. The mutations of the programming intents represent possible corner cases and misunderstandings of the program behavior, i.e., program specifications, and thus can capture different classes of faults than traditional (syntax-based) mutation. Moreover, since programming intents can be implemented in different ways, intent-based mutation testing can generate diverse and complex mutations that are close to the original programming intents (specifications) and thus direct testing towards the intent variants of the program behavior/specifications. We implement intent-based mutation testing using Large Language Models (LLMs) that mutate programming intents and transform them into mutants. We evaluate intent-based mutation on 29 programs and show that it generates mutations that are syntactically complex, semantically diverse, and quite different (semantically) from the traditional ones. We also show that 55% of the intent-based mutations are not subsumed by traditional mutations. Overall, our analysis shows that intent-based mutation testing can be a powerful complement to traditional (syntax-based) mutation testing.

</details>


### [409] [Is Three the Magic Number? An Empirical Evaluation of LLM-Based Repair Loops](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05197)
*Tobias Kiecker,Eik Reichmann,Hosung Kang,Gabin An,Lars Grunske*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 该研究系统分析了LLM软件工程中修复循环的迭代次数限制，发现前3-4次修复贡献了大部分收益，后续迭代收益递减，且修复行为受工作流编排和反馈设计的影响大于底层模型本身。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管迭代修复循环已成为LLM软件工程系统的核心设计模式，但修复循环的迭代次数限制对效果的影响缺乏系统理解，现有研究多采用固定且任意的修复预算。

Method: 在代码生成、测试生成和代码翻译等多个软件工程任务中，使用多种代表性工作流、数据集和当代低成本LLM，系统研究修复循环的有效性。

Result: 发现收益递减的一致模式：前3-4次迭代贡献了大部分可获得的收益，后续迭代仅带来边际改进；修复行为受工作流编排和反馈设计的影响大于底层模型。

Conclusion: 修复预算应被视为明确的实验变量，因为它直接影响LLM软件工程研究中的评估结果、计算成本、运行时间和可重复性。

Abstract: Iterative repair loops have become a core design pattern in LLM-based software engineering systems. These workflows repeatedly generate, validate, and repair artifacts using feedback such as compiler errors or test failures. Despite their widespread use, the impact of repair-loop iteration limits remains poorly understood, as most prior work adopts fixed, often arbitrary, repair budgets. We study repair-loop effectiveness across multiple software engineering tasks, including code generation, test generation, and code translation. Across several representative workflows, datasets, and contemporary low-cost LLMs, we observe a consistent pattern of diminishing returns: the first three to four repair iterations account for most achievable gains, while later iterations contribute only marginal improvements. We further find that repair behavior is influenced more strongly by workflow orchestration and feedback design than by the underlying model itself. These results suggest that repair budgets should be treated as an explicit experimental variable, as they directly affect evaluation outcomes, computational cost, runtime, and reproducibility in LLM-based software engineering research.

</details>


### [410] [An Investigation of the AUTOSAR Adaptive Platform from an Industry Perspective](https://arxiv.org/abs/2607.05227)
*Bengt Haraldsson,Srijita Basu,Miroslaw Staron,Erika Mayer*

Main category: cs.SE

TL;DR: 本文通过设计科学研究，开发最小化AUTOSAR Adaptive平台原型，发现规范本身、供应商实现和本地实践三方面因素共同导致开发痛点，建议通过改进工具配置管理和减少培训时间来缓解。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 汽车行业对软件的依赖日益增加，AUTOSAR Adaptive Platform（AP）旨在提供高性能面向服务的架构，但其实际开发中存在的痛点尚不明确，本研究旨在探究这些痛点及其根源。

Method: 采用设计科学研究（DSR）方法，开发一个最小化AP原型作为实验平台，系统性地分析痛点来源于平台规范、供应商实现还是本地使用实践。

Result: 发现规范本身、基于实现的因素以及本地实践三方面的共同作用导致了痛点的出现。

Conclusion: AUTOSAR规范的架构选择与复用目标是痛点产生的内在原因；开发组织应通过优化配置管理工具和减少开发者对自适应应用运行时生命周期的培训时间来缓解这些问题。

Abstract: The reliance on software as a distinguishing factor in the automotive industry is increasing. With a combined reliance on vendor-supplied software and cost-effective implementation, the AUTOSAR consortium was initialized to provide standardized platform specifications that enable re-use. Specifically, the AUTOSAR Adaptive Platform (AP) specification aims to provide a high-performance service-oriented architecture.
  Objective: The goal of this study is to investigate what pain-points emerge when developing AUTOSAR Adaptive applications and whether they originate from the platform specification, its vendor-implementation, or its local usage. Methods: We conduct a Design Science Research study, developing a minimal AP that serves as an experimental prototype for our investigation.
  Results: We find that a combination of specification-inherent, implementation-based, and local practices contributes to the emergence of pain-points.
  Conclusions: We conclude that there are AUTOSAR specification-inherent reasons for pain-points, resulting from architectural choices and re-use goals. The implication for development organizations is the need to mitigate these effects through tooling that better supports configuration file management and reduces developer training time to properly understand the adaptive application runtime life-cycle.

</details>
